		tile = {

					}
					AND = {
						has_food = yes
						has_minerals = no

					}
					has_deposit = no
				}

				any_neighboring_tile = {
					NOR = {

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic

	}

			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
				has_country_flag = synthetic_age
				OR = {
					has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
					has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 8
				unity = 2
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved
				OR = {
					has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
					has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
				}
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = is_food_starved
					has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
				}
			}
			resources = {
				minerals = 4
				unity = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_food_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1
	}
	planet_modifier = { pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.1 }
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	prerequisites = { "tech_planetary_government" }
	# Can't put more than one constraint on 'count' in a single 'count_xxx' statement, refactored to compensate
	
	potential = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			count_pops = {
				count > 4
				limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	destroy_if = {
		AND = {
			exists = owner
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_capital_2
	}
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }
  

	is_listed = no
}

				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 2
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
				NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine }
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
					has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				}
			}
			resources = {
				minerals = 2
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
					has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 2
				minerals = 1
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_energy_starved
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				NOT = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
			}
			resources = {
				minerals = 2
				unity = 1
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_machine_capital_1
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_energy = yes
						has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					}
					AND = {
						has_minerals = yes
						has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					}
					has_deposit = no
				}
				num_adjacent_tiles > 2
				any_neighboring_tile = {
					NOR = {
						has_hyperstorage_building = yes
						has_polytechnic_building = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_2
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_resource_machine = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { num_adjacent_tiles = 4 }
		}
	}

				NOT = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
			}
			resources = {
				minerals = 4
				unity = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1
	}

		building_machine_capital_2
	}

		"tech_planetary_government"
	}
	
	potential = {
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			count_pops = {
				count > 4
				limit = { is_colony_pop = yes }
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_colonial_centralization" }
			owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}

		exists = owner
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_energy = yes
						has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					}
					AND = {
						has_minerals = yes
						has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					}
					has_deposit = no
				}
				num_adjacent_tiles > 2
				any_neighboring_tile = {
					NOR = {
						has_hyperstorage_building = yes
						has_polytechnic_building = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_2
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_resource_machine = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { num_adjacent_tiles = 4 }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_machine_capital_1

building_hab_capital = {
	base_buildtime = @capital_build_time_tier_2
	planet_unique = yes
	capital = yes
	ai_replace = no
	cost = {}
	produced_resources = { }
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1
	}
	
	country_modifier = {
		max_energy = 1000
		max_minerals = 1000
	}
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			resources = { unity = 1	}
		}
		modifier = {
			and = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_authority = auth_hive_mind
						NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive }
					}
					NOR = {
						has_authority = auth_hive_mind
						has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
					}
				}
				NOR = {
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
					has_country_flag = "synthetic_age"
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
				food = 4
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
					NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine }
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = "synthetic_age"
					NOT = { has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever }
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
				minerals = 4
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			and = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_authority = auth_hive_mind
						has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_hive
					}
					AND = {
						NOR = {
							has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
							has_authority = auth_hive_mind
							has_country_flag = "synthetic_age"
						}
						has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
					}
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
				food = 4
				unity = 2
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
					has_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever_machine
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = "synthetic_age"
					has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_expansion_colonization_fever
				}
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 4
				minerals = 4
				unity = 2
			}
		}
	}
	planet_modifier = {	pop_government_ethic_attraction = 0.15 }
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_planet_class = pc_habitat
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_capital_3
		building_machine_capital_3
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			AND = {
				has_deposit = no
				num_adjacent_tiles > 2
				any_neighboring_tile = {
					NOR = {
						has_hyperstorage_building = yes
						has_polytechnic_building = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_2
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_resource_machine = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { num_adjacent_tiles = 4 }
		}
	}
}

	}

					any_neighboring_tile = { NOT = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_2
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				has_non_sapient_robot = yes
			}
		}

building_akx_worm_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @planet_unique_build_time_2
	planet_unique = yes
	ai_replace = no
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_build_cost_2
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_build_cost_2
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_capital_1 = yes
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
				has_building = "building_hab_capital"
			}
			NOR = {
				has_building = "building_power_hub_1"
				has_building_power_hub_2 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	planet_modifier = {
		tile_resource_energy_mult = 0.20
		pop_happiness = -0.05
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = @planet_unique_output_3 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_akx_worm_1"	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_energy = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_energy = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = "building_sr_engos_2" } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

				OR = {
					has_society = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes

					}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_sociologists" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife"
					has_modifier = "titanic_life"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1

				OR = {

			}
		}
		modifier = {

			guilli_society_modifiers = yes
		}
	}

			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2

		society_research = 2
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1
	}
	
	potential = {
		owner = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = "ex_traditions_active"
				has_swapped_tradition = tr_discovery_polytechnic_education_machine
			}
		}
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_building = "building_hab_capital"
				has_building_machine_capital_1 = yes
				has_building_machine_capital_2 = yes
				has_building = "building_machine_capital_3"
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_discovery_polytechnic_education_machine }
		}
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_1
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_research_resources = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_research_buildings = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_research_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife" # society
					has_modifier = "titanic_life" # society
					has_modifier = "unstable_tectonics" # engineering
					has_modifier = "wild_storms" # physics
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen" # society
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen_good" # society
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_engineering_modifiers = yes
				guilli_society_modifiers = yes
				guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_build_cost_2
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_build_cost_2
	}

	required_resources = { energy = @planet_unique_upkeep_2	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_cloning" }
	
	ai_allow = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = synthetic_age } }
		planet = { has_15_or_more_organic_pops = yes }
		is_slave_tile_or_planet = no
		is_robot_tile_or_planet = no
		tile = {
			OR = {
				has_deposit = no
				AND = {
					has_food = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @avoid
		modifier = {
			weight = @good
			owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_armies_active" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = "ex_armies_active"
					has_technology = "tech_morphogenetic_field_mastery"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			owner = {
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = "ex_armies_active"
					has_technology = "tech_gene_seed_purification"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = { has_trait = "trait_strong" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = { has_trait = "trait_very_strong" }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
building_slave_processing = {
	base_buildtime = @planet_unique_build_time_2
	planet_unique = yes
	ai_replace = no
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_build_cost_2
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_build_cost_2
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_output_1
		food = @planet_unique_output_1
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @planet_unique_upkeep_2 }
	
	planet_modifier = {
		slave_mineral_output = 0.10
		slave_food_output = 0.10
		country_unrest_unhappy_slave_effect_mult = -0.50
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		owner = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
				has_policy_flag = slavery_allowed
			}
		}
		planet = {
			AND = {
				any_pop = { is_enslaved = yes }
				OR = {
					has_capital_1 = yes
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		AND = {
			exists = owner
			owner = {
				OR = {
					has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
					NOT = { has_policy_flag = slavery_allowed }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_neural_implants" }
	
	ai_allow = {
		planet = {
			count_pops = {
				limit = { is_enslaved = yes }
				count > 2
			}
		}
		tile = {
			OR = {
				has_deposit = no
				AND = {
					has_food = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_food = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_1 }
}

		}

	}

					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}

			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}

			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {

					has_high_food = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = "building_sr_engos_2" } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {

				AND = {

					}

				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}

		"tech_mineral_processing_2"
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @planet_unique_output_2 }
	planet_modifier = { tile_resource_minerals_mult = 0.20 }
	required_resources = { energy = 3 }
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
					has_high_food = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_robot_pop = yes
					has_slave_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
					has_modifier = "carbon_world"
					has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
					has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = {
					any_neighboring_tile = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_sr_ex_planetary_1"
							has_building = "building_sr_engos_2"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_mineral_processing_plant_2
	
	upgrades = {
		building_mineral_processing_plant_1_hidden_tree_root
	}
}

building_mineral_silo_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @planet_unique_build_time_1
	planet_unique = yes
	ai_replace = no
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_build_cost_1
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_build_cost_1
	}
	allow = { }
	
	country_modifier = {
		max_minerals = 1000
		max_energy = 1000
	}
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = synthetic_age
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 1
				food = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = synthetic_age
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
			}
			resources = {
				energy = 2
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1
		tile_building_resource_food_add = 1
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_hyperstorage_1" }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_mineral_silo_2
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					has_deposit = no
					has_energy = yes
					has_minerals = yes
					has_food = yes
				}
				has_research_resources = no
				any_neighboring_tile = {
					NOR = {
						has_capital_building = yes
						has_polytechnic_building = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { num_adjacent_tiles = 4  }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_resource_buildings = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_research_buildings = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
	}
	
	potential = {
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_hyperstorage_2" }
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_capital_1 = yes
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
					has_building = "building_hab_capital"
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					type = sr_alien_pets
					amount > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_alien_life_studies" }
	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }
}
building_basic_power_plant = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_0
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_0
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = { has_capital_0 = yes }
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_0 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_power_plant_1
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_energy = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_energy = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = "building_sr_engos_2" } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "solar_planet"
							has_modifier = "rift_planet"
						}
					}
				}
				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "golden_city" }
			}
		}
	}
}

	base_buildtime = 0
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 0
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_1 = yes
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_1 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_power_plant_2
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_power_plant_1" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important				
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = { 
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					has_energy_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
						has_robot_pop = yes						
					}					
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = building_sr_engos_2 }
					}					
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {

							has_modifier = "solar_planet"

		}

			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "golden_city" }
			}
		}
	}



	is_listed = no
}

building_power_plant_3 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_3
	cost = { minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_3 }
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_3 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_power_plant_4
		building_power_plant_rw
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_power_plant_3" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important				
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = { 
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					has_energy_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
						has_robot_pop = yes						
					}					
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = building_sr_engos_2 }
					}					
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "solar_planet"
							has_modifier = "rift_planet"
						}
					}
				}
				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "golden_city" }
			}
		}
	}



	is_listed = no
}
building_power_plant_rw_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 277
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 300
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_power_plant_4" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				is_capital = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_4.5 }
	adjacency_bonus = {	tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_power_plant_4"
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_power_plant_5_rw
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_energy = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_energy = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = "building_sr_engos_2" } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_energy_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_power_plant_rw
}
building_power_plant_rw = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	cost = { minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5 }
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_4.5 }
	adjacency_bonus = {	tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_power_plant_4" }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_power_plant_5_rw
	}
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }
	
	
	is_listed = no
}

	cost = {

			factor = @good

					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}

					type = energy

				}
			}
		}

				has_slave_pop = yes

					has_non_sapient_robot = yes

			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1

		}

	prerequisites = {
		"tech_power_plant_4"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_energy = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_energy = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = "building_sr_engos_2" } }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_energy_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "solar_planet"
							has_modifier = "rift_planet"
						}
					}
				}
				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "golden_city" }
			}
		}
	}
	icon = building_power_plant_5
}
building_power_plant_5 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	cost = { minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5 }
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_5 }
	adjacency_bonus = {	tile_building_resource_energy_add = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_power_plant_4" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important				
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = { 
					owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
					has_energy_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
						has_robot_pop = yes						
					}					
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_building = building_sr_engos_2 }
					}					
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "strong_magnetic_field" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "hazardous_weather" }
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "solar_planet"
							has_modifier = "rift_planet"
						}
					}
				}
				guilli_energy_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_energy_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "golden_city" }
			}
		}
	}



	is_listed = no
}
building_basic_farm = {
	tags = { hydroponics_farm }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_0
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_0
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_0
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		planet = { has_capital_0 = yes }
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	produced_resources = { food = @resource_building_output_tier_0 }
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = {
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_0 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_hydroponics_farm_1
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			NOR = {
				has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = yes
				has_research_resources = yes
				has_minerals = yes
				has_energy = yes
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = "irradiated_planet"
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = "legw_active"
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "lava_planet"
						has_modifier = "art_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_slave_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "eat_the_titans" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_food = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}
	}
}

					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_slave_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "eat_the_titans" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_food = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_hydroponics_farm_2
}

		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }

		}

			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish

			}

					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes

			}

				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
				guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}
	}

			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }

				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_nano_vitality_crops" }
			owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
			planet = {
				is_ringworld_or_machine_world = no
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				OR = {
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
			planet = {
				is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes
				OR = {
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	}

		building_hydroponics_farm_4
		building_hydroponics_farm_rw
	}

		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	produced_resources = { food = @resource_building_output_tier_3 }

		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = { unity = 1	}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = { minerals = 1 }
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_3 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_gene_crops"
	}

		tile = {
			NOR = {
				has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = yes
				has_research_resources = yes
				has_minerals = yes
				has_energy = yes
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = "irradiated_planet"
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = "legw_active"
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "lava_planet"
						has_modifier = "art_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {

					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_slave_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {

	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_food_add = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_nano_vitality_crops" }
	ai_allow = {
		tile = { has_building = building_basic_farm }   
	} 

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { 
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_food_bonus_pop = yes
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } 
					any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }
				}
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
				guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}
	}



	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }
	
	
	is_listed = no
}
building_hydroponics_farm_4_direct_build = {
	tags = { hydroponics_farm }
	base_buildtime = 269
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 280
		#energy = 280
	}
	
	potential = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = no
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_nano_vitality_crops" }
			owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				is_capital = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_hydroponics_farm_5
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
	}
	produced_resources = { food = @resource_building_output_tier_4 }
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = {
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_4 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_nano_vitality_crops"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			NOR = {
				has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = yes
				has_research_resources = yes
				has_minerals = yes
				has_energy = yes
			}
		}
		planet = {
			NOT = {
				has_modifier = "irradiated_planet"
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = "legw_active"
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "lava_planet"
						has_modifier = "art_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_slave_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "eat_the_titans" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_food = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_hydroponics_farm_4
}

					has_global_flag = "legw_active"
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "lava_planet"
						has_modifier = "art_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_slave_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_food_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "eat_the_titans" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_food = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}
	}
	icon = building_hydroponics_farm_5

building_hydroponics_farm_5 = {
	tags = { hydroponics_farm }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_5
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
	
	potential = {
		owner = { NOT = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	allow = {  }
	
	destroy_if = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				exists = owner
				owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
			}
			planet = { is_capital = no }
		}
	}
	produced_resources = { food = @resource_building_output_tier_5 }
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			NOT = { has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish }
			resources = {
				unity = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll }
			resources = {
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			has_swapped_tradition = tr_adaptability_finish
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
			resources = {
				unity = 1
				minerals = 1
			}
		}
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_nano_vitality_crops" }
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_food_add = 1 }
	ai_allow = {
		tile = { has_building = building_basic_farm }   
	} 

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { 
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes

					any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }
				}
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
				guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }

			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }

building_basic_mine = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_0
	
	potential = {
		planet = { has_capital_0 = yes }
	}
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_0
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_0
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_0 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_0 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_mining_network_1
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_minerals = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "mineral_poor" }
				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_robot_pop = yes
					has_slave_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = {
					any_neighboring_tile = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_sr_ex_planetary_1"
							has_building = "building_sr_engos_2"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
					has_modifier = "carbon_world"
					has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
					has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

		#energy = 0
	}

				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = {
					OR = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						has_slave_pop = yes
						has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes				
						has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }						
						AND = {
							owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
							tile = {
								any_neighboring_tile = {
									OR = {
										has_building = building_sr_ex_planetary_1
										has_building = building_sr_engos_2
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}	
				}	
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
						has_modifier = "carbon_world"
						has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
						has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
					}
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {

				planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }

				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}

			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_mining_network_2
}
building_mining_network_2 = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_2
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_1 = yes
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_2
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_2
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_2 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_2 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_mining_network_3
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_mining_network_2" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "mineral_poor" }
				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = {
					OR = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						has_slave_pop = yes
						has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes				
						has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }						
						AND = {
							owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
							tile = {
								any_neighboring_tile = {
									OR = {
										has_building = building_sr_ex_planetary_1
										has_building = building_sr_engos_2
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}	
				}	
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
						has_modifier = "carbon_world"
						has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
						has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
					}
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" } 
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no
}
building_mining_network_3_direct_build = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = 202
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_mining_network_4" }
			planet = {
				is_ringworld_or_machine_world = no
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				OR = {
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
			planet = {
				is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes
				OR = {
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 180
		#energy = 180
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_3 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_3 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_mining_network_4
		building_mining_network_rw
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_mining_network_3"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_minerals = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "mineral_poor" }
				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_robot_pop = yes
					has_slave_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = {
					any_neighboring_tile = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_sr_ex_planetary_1"
							has_building = "building_sr_engos_2"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
					has_modifier = "carbon_world"
					has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
					has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1

				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no

	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = 344
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 400
		#energy = 400
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no }	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_5 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_mining_network_4"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_minerals = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_minerals = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "mineral_poor" }
				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_robot_pop = yes
					has_slave_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
				tile = {
					any_neighboring_tile = {
						OR = {
							has_building = "building_sr_ex_planetary_1"
							has_building = "building_sr_engos_2"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
					has_modifier = "carbon_world"
					has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
					has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_mineral_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_mining_network_5
}

building_mining_network_5 = {
	tags = { mining_network }
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_5
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	allow = {  }
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no }	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_5 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_minerals_add = 1 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_mining_network_4" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "mineral_poor" }
				guilli_negative_mineral_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = {
					OR = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						has_slave_pop = yes
						has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes				
						has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes }
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes }						
						AND = {
							owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_resources_active" }
							tile = {
								any_neighboring_tile = {
									OR = {
										has_building = building_sr_ex_planetary_1
										has_building = building_sr_engos_2
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}	
				}	
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "extensive_moon_system"
						has_modifier = "carbon_world"
						has_modifier = "mineral_rich"
						has_modifier = "asteroid_belt"
					}
				}					
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "ultra_rich" } 
				guilli_positive_mineral_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "lava_planet"
							has_modifier = "mine_cold"
							has_modifier = "auto_mining"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_minerals_starved }
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no
}
building_basic_science_lab_1 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_1
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_1
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_1
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_engineering_lab_1" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				OR = {
					has_capital_1 = yes
					has_capital_2 = yes
					has_capital_3 = yes
				}
			}
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_physics_lab_1" }
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_biolab_1" }
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_1 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_engineering_facility_1
		building_physics_lab_1
		building_biolab_1
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_basic_science_lab_1" }
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {
						OR = {
							has_trait = "trait_natural_engineers"
							has_trait = "trait_natural_physicists"
							has_trait = "trait_natural_sociologists"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife" # society
					has_modifier = "titanic_life" # society
					has_modifier = "unstable_tectonics" # engineering
					has_modifier = "wild_storms" # physics
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen" # society
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen_good" # society
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_engineering_modifiers = yes
				guilli_society_modifiers = yes
				guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "art_planet"
							has_modifier = "core_planet"
							has_modifier = "timeshift_slow"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = { has_trait = "trait_natural_engineers" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = { has_modifier = "unstable_tectonics" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_engineering_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "art_planet"
							has_modifier = "core_planet"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_engineering_facility_1
}
