building_engineering_facility_4_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 344
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 400
		#energy = 400
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_5
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_engineering_research_add = 1 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_engineering_lab_3"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_research_buildings = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = { has_trait = "trait_natural_engineers" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = { has_modifier = "unstable_tectonics" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_engineering_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "art_planet"
							has_modifier = "core_planet"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_engineering_facility_4
}

					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_physicists" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = { has_modifier = "wild_storms" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "core_planet"
							has_modifier = "timeshift_slow"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}

building_physics_lab_2 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_3
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_3
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_3
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_2
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_3 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_physics_lab_3
		building_physics_lab_rw
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_physics_lab_2" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = {
					OR = {
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes }
						has_research_bonus_pop = yes
						has_free_sapient_robot = yes
						AND = {
							exists = pop
							pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_physicists" }
						}
					}	
				}
				planet = { has_modifier = "wild_storms" }
				OR = {
					guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
						planet = {
							OR = {
								has_modifier = "core_planet"
								has_modifier = "timeshift_slow"
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no
}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2

		}

			tile = {

					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop

				}
			}

			guilli_physics_modifiers = yes

	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_5
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	
	adjacency_bonus = {
		tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 2
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_physics_lab_3"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_physics_research_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_physicists" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = { has_modifier = "wild_storms" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
				AND = {
					owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
					planet = {
						OR = {
							has_modifier = "core_planet"
							has_modifier = "timeshift_slow"
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	icon = building_physics_lab_4
}
building_physics_lab_4 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_5
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_5
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
	}
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_physics_research_add = 1 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_physics_lab_3" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = {
					OR = {
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes }
						has_research_bonus_pop = yes
						has_free_sapient_robot = yes
						AND = {
							exists = pop
							pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_physicists" }
						}
					}	
				}
				planet = { has_modifier = "wild_storms" }
				OR = {
					guilli_physics_modifiers = yes
					AND = {
						owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
						planet = {
							OR = {
								has_modifier = "core_planet"
								has_modifier = "timeshift_slow"
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
						has_modifier = "rift_planet"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no
}

building_biolab_rw = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_5
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_5
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_5
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_4
	}
	adjacency_bonus = { tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	prerequisites = { "tech_biolab_3" }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_biolab_4_rw
	}
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }
	
	
	is_listed = no
}
building_biolab_3_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 269
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 280
		#energy = 280
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = no
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
		NAND = {
			owner = { has_technology = "tech_biolab_3" }
			planet = {
				NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
				is_capital = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_3
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_4 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_biolab_4
	}
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_biolab_3"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_sociologists" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife"
					has_modifier = "titanic_life"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen"
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen_good"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			guilli_society_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_biolab_3
}
building_biolab_3 = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_4
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_4
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_tier_4
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_ringworld_or_machine_world = no
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			OR = {
				has_capital_2 = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_3
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_4 }
	
	upgrades = {
		building_biolab_4
	}
	prerequisites = { "tech_biolab_3" }
	ai_allow = { always = yes }
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @important
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				tile = { 
					OR = {
						any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } 
						has_research_bonus_pop = yes
						has_free_sapient_robot = yes
						AND = {
							exists = pop
							pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_sociologists" }
						}	
					}	
				}
			}
			guilli_society_modifiers = yes
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife"
					has_modifier = "titanic_life"
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen"
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen_good"					
				}
			}							
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	

	is_listed = no
}
building_biolab_4_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 344
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 400
		#energy = 400
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_habitat }
			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }
	
	produced_resources = {
		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		society_research = @resource_building_output_tier_5
	}
	adjacency_bonus = {	tile_building_resource_society_research_add = 1 }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_tier_5 }
	
	prerequisites = {
		"tech_biolab_3"
	}
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = { has_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = { has_high_research_resources = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_resources = no
					AND = {
						owner_is_not_machine_or_is_servitor = yes
						has_high_food = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @avoid
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_slave_pop = yes
					has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_polytechnic_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_society_research_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_research_bonus_pop = yes
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				AND = {
					exists = pop
					pop = {	has_trait = "trait_natural_sociologists" }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "dangerous_wildlife"
					has_modifier = "titanic_life"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			planet = {
				OR = {
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen"
					has_modifier = "atmospheric_hallucinogen_good"
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			guilli_society_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = {
					OR = {
						has_modifier = "ancient_planet"
						has_modifier = "timeshift_fast"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	show_tech_unlock_if = { always = no }
	icon = building_biolab_4
}
building_biolab_4_rw_direct_build = {
	base_buildtime = 352
	
	cost = {
		minerals = 420
		#energy = 420
	}
	
	potential = {

			is_capital = yes
			has_capital_3 = yes
		}
		planet = { is_ringworld_or_machine_world = yes }
	}
	
	allow = {
	}
	destroy_if = { planet = { is_capital = no } }

		engineering_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0
		physics_research = @resource_building_output_tier_0

						has_free_sapient_robot = yes

							exists = pop

building_hab_astro_mining_facility = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_4
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_4
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_hab
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_planet_class = pc_habitat
			has_building = "building_hab_capital"
		}
		NAND = {
			planet = {
				is_planet_class = pc_habitat
				is_capital = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_hab_astro_mining_facility_2
	}
	produced_resources = { minerals = @resource_building_output_tier_hab }
	required_resources = { energy = @resource_building_upkeep_hab }
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				has_minerals = yes
				AND = {
					has_energy = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = minerals
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_robot_pop = yes
					has_slave_pop = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_mineral_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1

		}

			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }

building_hab_solar_power_processor = {
	base_buildtime = @resource_building_build_time_tier_4
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @basic_resource_building_cost_4
		#energy = @resource_building_energy_cost_hab
	}
	
	potential = {
		planet = {
			is_planet_class = pc_habitat
			has_building = "building_hab_capital"
			no_black_hole_or_dyson_sphere_star = yes
		}
		NAND = {
			planet = {
				is_planet_class = pc_habitat
				is_capital = yes
				has_capital_3 = yes
				no_black_hole_or_dyson_sphere_star = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	upgrades = {
		building_hab_solar_power_processor_2
	}
	destroy_if = { no_black_hole_or_dyson_sphere_star = no }
	produced_resources = { energy = @resource_building_output_tier_hab }
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				has_energy = yes
				AND = {
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @standard
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { owner = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence } }
		}
	}
}

building_paradise_dome = {
	base_buildtime = @planet_unique_build_time_3
	planet_unique = yes
	ai_replace = no
	
	cost = {
		minerals = @planet_unique_mineral_cost_3
		energy = @planet_unique_energy_cost_3
	}
	required_resources = { energy = @planet_unique_upkeep_3	}
	produced_resources = { unity = 3 }
	
	produced_resource_trigger = {
		modifier = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = synthetic_age }
			resources = { food = 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			has_country_flag = synthetic_age
			resources = { energy = 3 }
		}
	}
	planet_modifier = { pop_citizen_happiness = 0.05 }
	
	potential = {
		owner = {	has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_harmony_utopian_dream }
		planet = {
			OR = {
				has_building = "building_hab_capital"
				has_building_capital_1 = yes
				has_building_capital_2 = yes
				has_building = "building_capital_3"
			}
		}
	}
	
	destroy_if = {
		exists = owner
		owner = {
			OR = {
				has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence
				NOT = { has_non_swapped_tradition = tr_harmony_utopian_dream }
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }
	
	ai_allow = {
		tile = {
			OR = {
				has_deposit = no
				NOR = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = yes
					has_research_resources = yes
					has_minerals = yes
					has_energy = yes
				}
			}
		}
		planet = { NOT = { has_modifier = "irradiated_planet" } }
		#owner = { NOT = { has_all_traditions = yes } }
	}
	
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @crucial_2
		modifier = {
			factor = @good
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @important
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = food
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_food_bonus_pop = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_hyperstorage_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { any_neighboring_tile = { has_capital_building = yes } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_2
			OR = {
				planet = { has_modifier = "lush_planet" }
				guilli_positive_food_modifiers = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_3
			planet = { has_modifier = "eat_the_titans" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			planet = { has_modifier = "bleak_planet" }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			guilli_negative_food_modifiers = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = { has_food = no }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_1
			owner = { has_country_flag = is_food_starved }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @crucial_2
			AND = {
				owner = { has_global_flag = "legw_active" }
				planet = { has_modifier = "food_corn" }
			}
		}

				}
				AND = {
					has_vanilla_or_exoverhaul_strategic_resources = no
					has_energy = no
					has_minerals = no
					has_research_resources = no
				}
			}
		}

					amount = 1

		}

			factor = @important

				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount = 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @strategic
			tile = {
				has_resource = {
					type = energy
					amount > 2
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					has_energy = no
					has_high_food = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @reduce_interest_2
			tile = {
				has_slave_pop = yes
				has_prole_or_stapled_pop = yes
				AND = {
					has_non_sapient_robot = yes
					exists = owner
					owner = { NOT = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" } }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = { has_energy_bonus_pop = yes	}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1
			tile = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_robot_pop = yes
						exists = owner
						owner = { has_global_flag = "ex_robots_active" }
					}
					has_free_sapient_robot = yes
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = @increase_interest_1

		modifier = {

					has_building_capital_1 = yes

			}

				is_spiritualist = no
				#has_all_traditions = yes
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { }

	ai_weight = { weight = @crucial_2 }

	is_listed = no
}
